  ensures d != 0 ==> -1000 <= d <= 1000
                      && CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) >= CeilHalf(|a|)

{

  var pcount := 0;
  var ncount := 0;
  var zcount := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant pcount == CountPositive(a[..i])
    invariant ncount == CountNegative(a[..i])
  {
    if a[i] > 0 {
      pcount := pcount + 1;
    } else if a[i] < 0 {

    i := i + 1;

       + (if IsPositiveAfterDiv(a[|a|-1], d) then 1 else 0)
}

ghost function CeilHalf(n: int): int
{
  (n + 1) / 2
}

ghost function CountPositive(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0
  else CountPositive(a[..|a|-1]) + (if a[|a|-1] > 0 then 1 else 0)

  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0
  else CountNegative(a[..|a|-1]) + (if a[|a|-1] < 0 then 1 else 0)
}

lemma CountPosDivPos(a: seq<int>, d: int)
  requires d > 0
  ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountPositive(a)
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| > 0 {
    CountPosDivPos(a[..|a|-1], d);
  }
}

lemma CountPosDivNeg(a: seq<int>, d: int)
  requires d < 0
  ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountNegative(a)
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| > 0 {
    CountPosDivNeg(a[..|a|-1], d);
  }
}

method BePositive(a: seq<int>) returns (d: int)
  ensures d != 0 ==> -1000 <= d <= 1000
                      && CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) >= CeilHalf(|a|)
  ensures d == 0 ==> (forall d' :: d' == 0 || CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|))
{
  var n := |a|;
  var pcount := 0;
  var ncount := 0;
  var zcount := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant pcount == CountPositive(a[..i])
    invariant ncount == CountNegative(a[..i])
    invariant zcount == |{j :: 0 <= j < i && a[j] == 0}|
    invariant |a[..i]| == i
  {
    if a[i] > 0 {
      pcount := pcount + 1;
    } else if a[i] < 0 {
      ncount := ncount + 1;
    } else {
      zcount := zcount + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  var half := (n + 1) / 2;
  if pcount >= half {
    d := 1;
    CountPosDivPos(a, 1);
  } else if ncount >= half {
    d := -1;
    CountPosDivNeg(a, -1);
  } else {
    d := 0;
    forall d' | d' != 0
      ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|)
    {
      if d' > 0 {
        CountPosDivPos(a, d');
      } else {
        CountPosDivNeg(a, d');
      }
    }
  }
}

    invariant pcount == CountPositive(a[..i])

  {

      pcount := pcount + 1;
    } else if a[i] < 0 {
      ncount := ncount + 1;
    } else {
      zcount := zcount + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;

                      && CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) >= CeilHalf(|a|)
  ensures d == 0 ==> (forall d' :: d' == 0 || CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|))
{
  var n := |a|;
  var pcount := 0;
  var ncount := 0;
  var zcount := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant pcount == CountPositive(a[..i])
    invariant ncount == CountNegative(a[..i])
  {
    if a[i] > 0 {
      pcount := pcount + 1;
    } else if a[i] < 0 {
      ncount := ncount + 1;
    } else {
      zcount := zcount + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  var half := (n + 1) / 2;
  if pcount >= half {
    d := 1;
    assert d > 0;
    CountPosDivPos(a, d);
  } else if ncount >= half {
    d := -1;
    assert d < 0;
    CountPosDivNeg(a, d);
  } else {
    d := 0;
    forall d' | d' != 0
      ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|)
    {
      if d' > 0 {
        CountPosDivPos(a, d');
      } else {
        CountPosDivNeg(a, d');
      }
    }
  }
}

    invariant pcount == CountPositive(a[..i])
    invariant ncount == CountNegative(a[..i])
  {
    if a[i] > 0 {
      pcount := pcount + 1;
    } else if a[i] < 0 {

  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0
  else CountNegative(a[..|a|-1]) + (if a[|a|-1] < 0 then 1 else 0)

  requires d > 0
  ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountPositive(a)
  decreases |a|
{

    CountPosDivPos(a[..|a|-1], d);
  }

lemma CountPosDivNeg(a: seq<int>, d: int)
  requires d < 0
  ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountNegative(a)
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| > 0 {
    CountPosDivNeg(a[..|a|-1], d);
  }
}

method BePositive(a: seq<int>) returns (d: int)
  ensures d != 0 ==> -1000 <= d <= 1000
                      && CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) >= CeilHalf(|a|)
  ensures d == 0 ==> (forall d' :: d' == 0 || CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|))
{
  var n := |a|;
  var pcount := 0;
  var ncount := 0;
  var zcount := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant pcount == CountPositive(a[..i])
    invariant ncount == CountNegative(a[..i])
  {
    if a[i] > 0 {
      pcount := pcount + 1;
    } else if a[i] < 0 {
      ncount := ncount + 1;
    } else {
      zcount := zcount + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  var half := (n + 1) / 2;
  if pcount >= half {
    d := 1;
    CountPosDivPos(a, 1);
  } else if ncount >= half {
    d := -1;
    CountPosDivNeg(a, -1);
  } else {
    d := 0;
    forall d' :: d' != 0
      ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|)
    {
      if d' > 0 {
        CountPosDivPos(a, d');
      } else {
        CountPosDivNeg(a, d');
      }
    }
  }
}

  (x > 0 && d > 0) || (x < 0 && d < 0)
}

ghost function CountPositiveAfterDiv(a: seq<int>, d: int): int
  requires d != 0
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0
  else CountPositiveAfterDiv(a[..|a|-1], d)
       + (if IsPositiveAfterDiv(a[|a|-1], d) then 1 else 0)
}

ghost function CeilHalf(n: int): int
{
  (n + 1) / 2
}

ghost function CountPositive(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0
  else CountPositive(a[..|a|-1]) + (if a[|a|-1] > 0 then 1 else 0)
}

ghost function CountNegative(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0
  else CountNegative(a[..|a|-1]) + (if a[|a|-1] < 0 then 1 else 0)
}

lemma CountPosDivPos(a: seq<int>, d: int)
  requires d > 0
  ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountPositive(a)
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| > 0 {
    CountPosDivPos(a[..|a|-1], d);
  }
  assert CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountPositive(a);
}

lemma CountPosDivNeg(a: seq<int>, d: int)
  requires d < 0
  ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountNegative(a)
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| > 0 {
    CountPosDivNeg(a[..|a|-1], d);
  }
  assert CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountNegative(a);
}

method BePositive(a: seq<int>) returns (d: int)
  ensures d != 0 ==> -1000 <= d <= 1000
                      && CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) >= CeilHalf(|a|)
  ensures d == 0 ==> (forall d' :: d' == 0 || CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|))
{
  var n := |a|;
  var pcount := 0;
  var ncount := 0;
  var zcount := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant pcount == CountPositive(a[..i])
    invariant ncount == CountNegative(a[..i])
  {
    if a[i] > 0 {
      pcount := pcount + 1;
    } else if a[i] < 0 {
      ncount := ncount + 1;
    } else {
      zcount := zcount + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  var half := (n + 1) / 2;
  if pcount >= half {
    d := 1;
    CountPosDivPos(a, 1);
  } else if ncount >= half {
    d := -1;
    CountPosDivNeg(a, -1);
  } else {
    d := 0;
    forall d' | d' != 0
      ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|)
    {
      if d' > 0 {
        CountPosDivPos(a, d');
      } else {
        CountPosDivNeg(a, d');
      }
    }
  }
}

    invariant pcount == CountPositive(a[..i])

  {

      pcount := pcount + 1;

method BePositive(a: seq<int>) returns (d: int)
  ensures d != 0 ==> -1000 <= d <= 1000
                      && CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) >= CeilHalf(|a|)
  ensures d == 0 ==> (forall d' :: d' == 0 || CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|))
{
  var n := |a|;
  var pcount := 0;
  var ncount := 0;
  var zcount := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant pcount == CountPositive(a[..i])
    invariant ncount == CountNegative(a[..i])
  {
    if a[i] > 0 {
      pcount := pcount + 1;
    } else if a[i] < 0 {
      ncount := ncount + 1;
    } else {
      zcount := zcount + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  var half := (n + 1) / 2;
  if pcount >= half {
    d := 1;
    assert CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountPositive(a);
    assert CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) >= CeilHalf(|a|) by {
      assert CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountPositive(a);
      assert CountPositive(a) >= CeilHalf(|a|) by {
        assert CountPositive(a) == pcount;
        assert pcount >= half;
        assert half == CeilHalf(|a|);
        assert CountPositive(a) >= CeilHalf(|a|);
      }
    }
  } else if ncount >= half {
    d := -1;
    assert CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountNegative(a);
    assert CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) >= CeilHalf(|a|) by {
      assert CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountNegative(a);
      assert CountNegative(a) >= CeilHalf(|a|) by {
        assert CountNegative(a) == ncount;
        assert ncount >= half;
        assert half == CeilHalf(|a|);
        assert CountNegative(a) >= CeilHalf(|a|);
      }
    }
  } else {
    d := 0;
    forall d' :: d' != 0
      ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|)
    {
      if d' > 0 {
        assert CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') == CountPositive(a);
        assert CountPositive(a) < CeilHalf(|a|) by {
          assert CountPositive(a) == pcount;
          assert pcount < half;
          assert half == CeilHalf(|a|);
          assert CountPositive(a) < CeilHalf(|a|);
        }
      } else {

        assert CountNegative(a) < CeilHalf(|a|) by {

          assert ncount < half;
          assert half == CeilHalf(|a|);
          assert CountNegative(a) < CeilHalf(|a|);
        }
      }
    }
  }

    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  var half := (n + 1) / 2;

      ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|)

      } else {
        CountPosDivNeg(a, d');
      }
    }

  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant pcount == CountPositive(a[..i])
    invariant ncount == CountNegative(a[..i])
  {
    if a[i] > 0 {
      pcount := pcount + 1;

       + (if IsPositiveAfterDiv(a[|a|-1], d) then 1 else 0)
}

ghost function CeilHalf(n: int): int
{
  (n + 1) / 2
}

ghost function CountPositive(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0
  else CountPositive(a[..|a|-1]) + (if a[|a|-1] > 0 then 1 else 0)
}

ghost function CountNegative(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0
  else CountNegative(a[..|a|-1]) + (if a[|a|-1] < 0 then 1 else 0)
}

lemma CountPosDivPos(a: seq<int>, d: int)
  requires d > 0
  ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountPositive(a)
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| > 0 {
    CountPosDivPos(a[..|a|-1], d);
  }
}

lemma CountPosDivNeg(a: seq<int>, d: int)
  requires d < 0
  ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountNegative(a)
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| > 0 {
    CountPosDivNeg(a[..|a|-1], d);
  }
}

method BePositive(a: seq<int>) returns (d: int)
  ensures d != 0 ==> -1000 <= d <= 1000
                      && CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) >= CeilHalf(|a|)
  ensures d == 0 ==> (forall d' :: d' == 0 || CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|))
{
  var n := |a|;
  var pcount := 0;
  var ncount := 0;
  var zcount := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant pcount == CountPositive(a[..i])
    invariant ncount == CountNegative(a[..i])
  {
    if a[i] > 0 {
      pcount := pcount + 1;
    } else if a[i] < 0 {
      ncount := ncount + 1;
    } else {
      zcount := zcount + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  var half := (n + 1) / 2;
  if pcount >= half {
    d := 1;
    assert CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountPositive(a);
    assert CountPositive(a) >= CeilHalf(|a|);
  } else if ncount >= half {
    d := -1;
    assert CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountNegative(a);
    assert CountNegative(a) >= CeilHalf(|a|);
  } else {
    d := 0;
    forall d' | d' != 0
      ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|)
    {
      if d' > 0 {
        assert CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') == CountPositive(a);
      } else {
        assert CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') == CountNegative(a);
      }
      assert CountPositive(a) < CeilHalf(|a|);
      assert CountNegative(a) < CeilHalf(|a|);
    }
  }
}

                      && CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) >= CeilHalf(|a|)

{
  var n := |a|;
  var pcount := 0;
  var ncount := 0;
  var zcount := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant pcount == CountPositive(a[..i])
    invariant ncount == CountNegative(a[..i])
  {
    if a[i] > 0 {
      pcount := pcount + 1;
    } else if a[i] < 0 {
      ncount := ncount + 1;
    } else {
      zcount := zcount + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  var half := (n + 1) / 2;
  if pcount >= half {
    d := 1;
    CountPosDivPos(a, 1);
    assert CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountPositive(a);
    assert CountPositive(a) >= CeilHalf(|a|); // because pcount >= half
  } else if ncount >= half {
    d := -1;

  requires d < 0
  ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountNegative(a)

    CountPosDivNeg(a[..|a|-1], d);

method BePositive(a: seq<int>) returns (d: int)
  ensures d != 0 ==> -1000 <= d <= 1000
                      && CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) >= CeilHalf(|a|)
  ensures d == 0 ==> (forall d' :: d' == 0 || CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|))
{
  var n := |a|;
  var pcount := 0;
  var ncount := 0;
  var zcount := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant pcount == CountPositive(a[..i])
    invariant ncount == CountNegative(a[..i])
  {
    if a[i] > 0 {
      pcount := pcount + 1;
    } else if a[i] < 0 {
      ncount := ncount + 1;
    } else {
      zcount := zcount + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  var half := (n + 1) / 2;
  if pcount >= half {
    d := 1;
    assert CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountPositive(a);
    assert CountPositive(a) >= CeilHalf(|a|); // from pcount >= half
  } else if ncount >= half {
    d := -1;
    assert CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountNegative(a);
    assert CountNegative(a) >= CeilHalf(|a|); // from ncount >= half
  } else {
    d := 0;
    forall d' | d' != 0
      ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|)
    {
      if d' > 0 {
        assert CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') == CountPositive(a);
        assert CountPositive(a) < CeilHalf(|a|); // by assumption of else branch
      } else {
        assert CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') == CountNegative(a);
        assert CountNegative(a) < CeilHalf(|a|); // by assumption of else branch
      }
    }
  }
}

ghost predicate IsPositiveAfterDiv(x: int, d: int)
  requires d != 0
{
  (x > 0 && d > 0) || (x < 0 && d < 0)
}

ghost function CountPositiveAfterDiv(a: seq<int>, d: int): int
  requires d != 0
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0
  else CountPositiveAfterDiv(a[..|a|-1], d)
       + (if IsPositiveAfterDiv(a[|a|-1], d) then 1 else 0)
}

ghost function CeilHalf(n: int): int
{
  (n + 1) / 2
}

ghost function CountPositive(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0
  else CountPositive(a[..|a|-1]) + (if a[|a|-1] > 0 then 1 else 0)
}

ghost function CountNegative(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0
  else CountNegative(a[..|a|-1]) + (if a[|a|-1] < 0 then 1 else 0)
}

lemma CountPosDivPos(a: seq<int>, d: int)
  requires d > 0
  ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountPositive(a)
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| > 0 {
    CountPosDivPos(a[..|a|-1], d);
  }
}

lemma CountPosDivNeg(a: seq<int>, d: int)
  requires d < 0
  ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountNegative(a)
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| > 0 {
    CountPosDivNeg(a[..|a|-1], d);
  }
}

method BePositive(a: seq<int>) returns (d: int)
  ensures d != 0 ==> -1000 <= d <= 1000
                      && CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) >= CeilHalf(|a|)
  ensures d == 0 ==> (forall d' :: d' == 0 || CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|))
{
  var n := |a|;
  var pcount := 0;
  var ncount := 0;
  var zcount := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant pcount == CountPositive(a[..i])
    invariant ncount == CountNegative(a[..i])
    invariant zcount == |a[..i]| - pcount - ncount
  {
    if a[i] > 0 {
      pcount := pcount + 1;
    } else if a[i] < 0 {
      ncount := ncount + 1;
    } else {
      zcount := zcount + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  var half := (n + 1) / 2;
  if pcount >= half {
    d := 1;
    assert CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountPositive(a); // lemma application
    assert CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) >= CeilHalf(|a|); // required by spec
  } else if ncount >= half {
    d := -1;
    assert CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountNegative(a); // lemma application
    assert CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) >= CeilHalf(|a|); // required by spec
  } else {
    d := 0;
    forall d' | d' != 0
      ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|)
    {
      if d' > 0 {
        assert CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') == CountPositive(a); // lemma application
        assert CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|); // required by spec
      } else {
        assert CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') == CountNegative(a); // lemma application
        assert CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|); // required by spec
      }
    }
  }
}
